	<div class="line t3">
		<div class="wp-block-jobber-academy-post-hero-ai-overview__summary-container">
			<div class="wp-block-jobber-academy-post-hero-ai-overview__summary">
				<h4 class="wp-block-jobber-academy-post-hero-ai-overview__summary-title">
					<svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">

					Key takeaways:
				</h4>
				<div class="wp-block-jobber-academy-post-hero-ai-overview__summary-content is-collapsed">
					<div class="wp-block-jobber-academy-post-hero-ai-overview__summary-content-loader">
						<div class="wp-block-jobber-academy-post-hero-ai-overview__summary-content-loading-bar gradient-1"></div>
						<div class="wp-block-jobber-academy-post-hero-ai-overview__summary-content-loading-bar gradient-2"></div>
						<div class="wp-block-jobber-academy-post-hero-ai-overview__summary-content-loading-bar gradient-3"></div>
					</div>
					<p>Figuring out how much to charge for house cleaning ensures your rates are both competitive and profitable.</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Base your pricing on service type, home size, and local rates.</strong> Basic house cleaning prices typically ranges from $20-50+ per hour, $100-200+ flat fee, $100-150+ per room, or $0.05-0.16+ per square foot.</li>
<li><strong>Charge appropriately for specialized services.</strong> Deep cleaning, move-out, construction cleanup, and specialty add-ons like laundry, appliance cleaning, and carpet cleaning command higher rates than standard cleaning jobs.</li>
<li><strong>Choose a pricing formula that fits your business.</strong> Select from hourly, flat rate, per-room, or per-square-foot pricing to match your level of experience, customer preferences, and predictability of each job.</li>
<li><strong>Factor in business costs for profitability.</strong> Always account for labor, materials, travel, overhead, and your desired profit margin when setting prices, and be ready to adjust as your business and market change.</li>
<li><strong>Keep pricing transparent and adaptable.</strong> Use a clear pricing sheet for customers and regularly review your rates as factors like home size, cleaning frequency, location, and competition affect your costs and opportunities.</li>
</ul>
<p>For more practical advice on pricing and growing your cleaning business, sign up for the Jobber Newsletter. <a href="https://www.getjobber.com/blueprint/#newsletter-signup" target="_blank">Sign up here.</a></p>
				</div>
			</div>
		</div>
	</div>
</section>

<section
	class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content t3 line--narrow-width
		  t3-margin-top-sm
		  
		  list-columns--one
		  "
	
>
	<div class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content__content">
		

<p>If youre ready to start cleaning houses professionally, the next step is determining what youll charge your clients. Pricing might feel overwhelming, especially if you offer a range of services.</p>



<p>Fortunately, industry benchmarks can help you create prices that are both competitive and profitable. According to Thumbtack, <a href="https://www.thumbtack.com/p/house-cleaning-prices" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener nofollow">house cleaners can charge</a>:</p>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li><strong>$45-50 per hour</strong>, based on the national average</li>



<li><strong>$175-$218 per home</strong> for low-end cleaning jobs</li>



<li><strong>$350-$400 per home</strong> for high-end cleaning jobs</li>
</ul>



<p>Whether youre looking for a quick reference on <a href="#how-much-to-charge">how much to charge for house cleaning</a>, want to learn <a href="#how-to-price">how to price out your services yourself</a>, or want to try our free <a href="#calculator">cleaning cost calculator</a>youve come to the right place.</p>



<p>In this house cleaning pricing guide, youll learn the best ways to charge for various house cleaning services to ensure that every job is profitable.</p>


	</div>
</section><!-- ./wp-block-jobber-academy-content -->

<h2 class="wp-block-heading" id="pricing-list">How much to charge for residential cleaning services (pricing chart)</h2>



<p>Heres how much you can typically charge for various <a href="https://www.getjobber.com/academy/cleaning/types-of-cleaning-services/">types of cleaning services</a>. In this chart, youll find calculations based on four different pricing structures:</p>

<section
	class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content t3 line--narrow-width
		  t3-margin-top-sm
		  
		  list-columns--one
		  u-anchor-offset"
	id="house-cleaning"
>
	<div class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content__content">
		

<h3 class="wp-block-heading">How much to charge for cleaning a house (standard residential cleaning)</h3>



<p>Standard house cleaning service includes tasks like dusting, wiping surfaces, vacuuming and mopping floors, and scrubbing bathroom fixtures.</p>



<p>Heres what your cleaning business can charge for general home cleaning tasks:</p>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li><strong>House cleaning hourly rate</strong>: $2050/hour per house cleaner, based on experience and team size</li>



<li><strong>Flat fee</strong>: $100170 weekly/biweekly for standard cleaning in a single-family home</li>



<li><strong>Room rate</strong>: $100 for 1 bed/1 bath + $1020 for each additional bedroom or bathroom</li>



<li><strong>Square footage rate</strong>: 515 per square foot for weekly or bi-weekly cleaning (note that the higher the square footage, the lower your rate should be)</li>
</ul>



<p><strong>PODCAST:</strong> <a href="https://www.getjobber.com/podcast/ep2-how-to-attract-high-paying-customers/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Listen and learn how to attract high-paying customers</a></p>


	</div>
</section><!-- ./wp-block-jobber-academy-content -->


<section
	class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content t3 line--narrow-width
		  t3-margin-top-sm
		  
		  list-columns--one
		  u-anchor-offset"
	id="deep-cleaning"
>
	<div class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content__content">
		

<h3 class="wp-block-heading">How much to charge for deep cleaning a house</h3>



<p>Deep cleaning involves a more thorough process than spot cleaning. This option might be recommended if the time between cleanings is more than several months.&nbsp;</p>



<p>With a deep clean, add an extra 3050% to your normal cleaning rates. There are several ways to price deep cleaning services for new and existing clients:</p>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li><strong>Deep clean hourly rate</strong>: $40100/hour per house cleaner, based on team size and experience</li>



<li><strong>Flat fee</strong>: $200400+, depending on the size of the home (and your team)</li>



<li><strong>Room rate</strong>: $125175 for a 3-bedroom, 2-bathroom home</li>



<li><strong>Square footage rate</strong>: $0.130.17 per sq ft (at the lower end for larger homes and the higher end for homes requiring more effort)</li>
</ul>


	</div>
</section><!-- ./wp-block-jobber-academy-content -->


<section
	class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content t3 line--narrow-width
		  t3-margin-top-sm
		  
		  list-columns--one
		  u-anchor-offset"
	id="move-out-cleaning"
>
	<div class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content__content">
		

<h3 class="wp-block-heading">How much to charge for move-out cleaning</h3>



<p>Move-out cleaning is another form of deep cleaning. However, the home is usually empty and free of furniture and clutter. When move-out cleaning is required (in a rental, lease, or purchase contingency), the cleaning must meet specific criteria. As a result, this one-time house cleaning cost could be:</p>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li><strong>Move-out cleaning hourly rate</strong>: $40100/hour per house cleaner</li>



<li><strong>Flat fee</strong>: $300400</li>



<li><strong>Room rate</strong>: $125175 for a 3-bedroom, 2-bathroom home</li>



<li><strong>Square footage rate</strong>: Up to $0.22 per square foot</li>
</ul>


	</div>
</section><!-- ./wp-block-jobber-academy-content -->


<section
	class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content t3 line--narrow-width
		  t3-margin-top-sm
		  
		  list-columns--one
		  u-anchor-offset"
	id="construction-cleanup"
>
	<div class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content__content">
		

<h3 class="wp-block-heading">How much to charge for construction cleanup</h3>



<p>Construction cleanup is similar to move-out cleaning because youre cleaning an empty space after a project. However, it may require a bit less elbow grease since the building is brand-new and free of furniture or other items.</p>



<p>Heres what your cleaning company could charge:</p>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li><strong>Construction cleanup hourly rate</strong>: $3050/hour per house cleaner</li>



<li><strong>Flat fee</strong>: Up to $800, depending on the size and condition of the space</li>



<li><strong>Room rate</strong>: $125175 for a 3-bedroom, 2-bathroom home</li>



<li><strong>Square footage rate</strong>: $0.100.50 per square foot</li>
</ul>


	</div>
</section><!-- ./wp-block-jobber-academy-content -->

<section
	class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content t3 line--narrow-width
		  t3-margin-top-sm
		  
		  list-columns--one

	id="specialty-services"

	<div class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content__content">
		

<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="h-how-much-to-charge-for-specialty-services-average-price-per-service">How much to charge for specialty services (average price per service)</h3>



<p>Specialty services are extra add-ons. These offerings can help clients solve other household problems when theyre low on time. Plus, theyre a chance for you to earn more per job.&nbsp;</p>



<p>Heres what you can charge for add-on cleaning tasks:</p>



<figure class="wp-block-table"><table class="has-fixed-layout"><thead><tr><th>Add-on house cleaning service</th><th>Average price per job</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Laundry</td><td>$520 per load (added fee for folding and putting away)</td></tr><tr><td>Appliance or oven cleaning</td><td>$2535+ per appliance (more if its in bad shape)</td></tr><tr><td>Blinds and window cleaning</td><td>$26 per window</td></tr><tr><td>Floor buffing</td><td>$0.040.12 per square foot</td></tr><tr><td>Tile cleaning</td><td>$0.120.21 per square foot</td></tr><tr><td>Carpet cleaning</td><td>$0.160.28 per square foot</td></tr><tr><td>Floor stripping and waxing</td><td>$0.300.50 per square foot</td></tr><tr><td>Furniture upholstery/curtain cleaning</td><td>$100+ per hour (depending on size, type, and condition)</td></tr><tr><td>Green cleaning supplies</td><td>$510 per cleaning job</td></tr><tr><td>Sanitization or odor removal services</td><td>$75-100 per hour</td></tr><tr><td>Ceiling and wall (paint) cleaning</td><td>$0.50 to $0.60 per square foot</td></tr><tr><td>Disaster or emergency restoration cleaning (i.e., water damage)</td><td>$1,000-4,000+</td></tr></tbody></table></figure>



<p><strong>READ MORE</strong>: <a href="https://www.getjobber.com/academy/good-better-best-pricing-examples/">Offer service packages with good, better, best pricing</a></p>



<p>Depending on your <a href="https://www.getjobber.com/academy/cleaning/professional-house-cleaning-checklist/">cleaning checklists</a>, some specialty services might already fall into basic house cleaning packages.&nbsp;</p>



<p>For example, youd probably wipe down a refrigerator during a normal house cleaning call. In other cases (especially if theres extra grime), you can charge additional fees for more labor.</p>


	</div>
</section><!-- ./wp-block-jobber-academy-content -->

<section
	class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content t3 line--narrow-width
		  t3-margin-top-sm
		  
		  list-columns--one
		  "
	
>
	<div class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content__content">
		

<p>Keep in mind that this pricing sheet is just a starting point. Set your own prices based on what feels right for your situation and your clientsand what theyre willing to pay.</p>



<p><em><strong>Pro Tip:</strong> </em>Set yourself apart from competitors with an eco-friendly <a href="https://www.getjobber.com/academy/cleaning/should-you-offer-green-cleaning-services/">green cleaning service</a>, either as a value add or an optional cost. Just make sure your bottom line can handle more expensive <a href="https://www.getjobber.com/academy/cleaning/cleaning-business-supplies-list/">cleaning supplies</a>.</p>


	</div>
</section><!-- ./wp-block-jobber-academy-content -->

<section

	<div class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content__content">
		

<h2 class="wp-block-heading" id="pricing-methods">How to price house cleaning services (pricing formulas)</h2>



<p>There are four options when deciding how to charge for house cleaning<a href="#hourly-pricing">hourly</a>, <a href="https://www.getjobber.com/academy/what-does-flat-rate-mean/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">flat rate</a>, <a href="#square-footage-pricing">square footage</a>, and <a href="#per-room">per room</a>. Each pricing method can be effective and profitable. Its simply a matter of finding the <a href="https://www.getjobber.com/academy/pricing-strategies-service-business/">pricing strategy</a> that works best for your personal and business goals.</p>



<p>In this video, our cleaning experts share how to properly charge for house cleaning services:</p>


	</div>
</section><!-- ./wp-block-jobber-academy-content -->

<section
	class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content t3 line--narrow-width
		  t3-margin-top-sm
		  
		  list-columns--one
		  u-anchor-offset"
	id="hourly-pricing"
>
	<div class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content__content">
		

<h3 class="wp-block-heading">1. Hourly pricing formula</h3>



<p>An<strong> hourly </strong>pricing model means youll charge customers a set rate for every working hour. This system ensures that you are compensated for your labor and time.</p>



<p>Heres how to price cleaning a house at an hourly rate, with an added 50% for <a href="https://www.getjobber.com/academy/overhead-costs/">overhead costs</a> and <a href="https://www.getjobber.com/academy/small-business-profit-margin-guide/">profit margin</a>:</p>



<p><strong>Hourly Rate</strong> = (Employees hourly wage x Number of employees) x 1.5</p>



<p>An appropriate hourly rate is $2550 for less experienced cleaners or standard services. A&nbsp;one-time deep cleaning cost per hour could be up to $100.</p>



<p><strong>Best Fit:</strong> When you arent sure how long a house cleaning job will take<br><strong>Poor Fit:</strong> Fast-working cleaners or clients who want a predictable fee for a single service</p>


	</div>
</section><!-- ./wp-block-jobber-academy-content -->


<section
	class="wp-block-jobber-t3-pullquote-testimonial t3
	t3-margin-top-sm
	line--narrow-width
	"
	
>
	<figure class="wp-block-jobber-t3-pullquote-testimonial__content bookend">
		<blockquote class="wp-block-jobber-t3-pullquote-testimonial__blockquote">
			<p class="wp-block-jobber-t3-pullquote-testimonial__quote">Charging per hour protects you from surprises, such as a client booking you for four hours if you go to the home and then you find out that the shower is going to take you four hours to clean. It&#8217;s a lesson learned.</p>
		</blockquote>

					

							<div class="wp-block-jobber-t3-pullquote-testimonial__author-container">
										<figcaption class="wp-block-jobber-t3-pullquote-testimonial__author">
						Latoya Barrington
													<span class="wp-block-jobber-t3-pullquote-testimonial__title"><a href="https://yourgo2girl.ca/">Go2Girl Services</a></span>
											</figcaption>
				</div>
						</figure>
</section><!-- ./wp-block-jobber-t3-pullquote-testimonial -->


<section
	class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content t3 line--narrow-width
		  t3-margin-top-sm
		  
		  list-columns--one
		  "
	
>
	<div class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content__content">
		

<p>Repeat clients might pay lower hourly cleaning rates since regular cleaning means less work each time. Charge a higher house cleaning rate if a home requires more effort or team members to get the job done.&nbsp;</p>



<p><strong><em>Pro Tip:</em></strong> Remember, if you have a variable hourly rate, you may not be able to advertise it widely to all new clients. Instead, you can market your services by encouraging prospects to contact you for a custom quote.</p>


	</div>
</section><!-- ./wp-block-jobber-academy-content -->


<section
	class="wp-block-jobber-academy-featured-content t3 line--narrow-width
	t3-margin-top-sm
	
	list-columns--one
	"
	
>
	<div class="wp-block-jobber-academy-featured-content__content">
		

<h3 class="wp-block-heading">How much do house cleaners make per hour?</h3>



<p>Housekeepers and house cleaners make <span style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://www.getjobber.com/resources/salary-guides/cleaner/" target="_blank"><strong>an average of $12/hour</strong></a></span> or $29,991/year. A cleaners actual hourly wage will vary depending on skill level, average pay in their state, and local cost of living.</p>


	</div>
</section><!-- ./wp-block-jobber-academy-featured-content -->


<section
	class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content t3 line--narrow-width
		  t3-margin-top-sm
		  
		  list-columns--one
		  u-anchor-offset"
	id="flat-rate"
>
	<div class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content__content">
		

<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="h-2-how-to-set-a-flat-rate-house-cleaning-price">2. How to set a flat rate house cleaning price</h3>



<p>A <strong>flat fee</strong> is determined by the amount of time you assume the job will take based on an estimate. For example, charging $175 to clean a two-bed, two-bath house. Flat fee pricing is helpful when youre juggling many recurring projects.</p>



<p><strong>Best Fit</strong>: Experienced cleaners and clients who want a predictable rate<br><strong>Poor Fit</strong>: Less experienced cleaners or jobs that require more time on-site</p>



<p>Flat fee pricing is one of the most common pricing methods for house cleanersand a favorite for clients. The budget is set from the start. This means that the faster you go, the more profit you take home.</p>



<p>There isnt a set formula for flat fee pricing because its based on value. However, you can typically charge $100170 per visit for cleaning a typical single-family home under 3,000 square feet. The cost can be higher for deep cleaning services or larger homes.</p>



<p>To set your house cleaning fee, consider average cost factors like:</p>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li>How long the job will take you or your employees</li>



<li>How many workers the job requires</li>



<li>Hourly overhead costs</li>



<li>A healthy <a href="https://www.getjobber.com/academy/cleaning/is-a-cleaning-business-profitable/">profit margin</a></li>



<li>Extra padding in case of delays (unexpected work in the home)</li>



<li>How much the client is willing to pay for convenience</li>
</ul>


	</div>
</section><!-- ./wp-block-jobber-academy-content -->


<section
	class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content t3 line--narrow-width
		  t3-margin-top-sm
		  
		  list-columns--one
		  u-anchor-offset"
	id="square-footage-pricing"
>
	<div class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content__content">
		

<h3 class="wp-block-heading">3. Square footage pricing formula</h3>



<p>In this model, charge customers a set rate per square foot of a home. Square footage pricing relies on an accurate measurement that you collect yourself or get from a homeowner.</p>



<p><strong>Best Fit</strong>: When you need to price multiple jobs quickly or <a href="https://www.getjobber.com/academy/cleaning/how-to-price-commercial-cleaning-jobs/">set commercial cleaning prices</a><strong> Poor Fit</strong>: First-time cleaning jobs when the scope of work is unknown</p>



<p>Some professional house cleaning companies set residential cleaning prices based on square footage. This type of pricing is easy to calculate on the spot when a client wants a quote based on the size of their space. Heres how to do it:</p>



<p><strong>Square Footage Cost</strong> = Homes square footage x Your cost per square foot</p>



<p>Charge a higher square footage rate for smaller spaces and less frequent, more detailed cleaning. For example:</p>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li>If youre deep cleaning a furnished 700-square-foot apartment at a square footage rate of 30, you would quote $210 for that one-time job.</li>



<li>Regularly cleaning a 2,000 sq ft home at a rate of 7 would earn you $140 each week. Its less income per job, but its recurring and predictable work.</li>
</ul>



<p>When you quote by square footage, run the numbers for a few different house sizes. Make sure each job is still profitable after deducting labor costs, <a href="https://www.getjobber.com/academy/cleaning/cleaning-business-supplies-list/">cleaning supplies</a>, and overhead.</p>


	</div>
</section><!-- ./wp-block-jobber-academy-content -->


<section
	class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content t3 line--narrow-width
		  t3-margin-top-sm
		  
		  list-columns--one
		  u-anchor-offset"
	id="per-room"
>
	<div class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content__content">
		

<h3 class="wp-block-heading">4. Per room pricing formula</h3>



<p>Per room pricing is a simple way to offer  la carte options to homeowners who dont want a full house package. You might price higher to compensate for cleaning less per trip.</p>



<p><strong>Best Fit</strong>: Repeat jobs where each room is in reasonably good condition<br><strong>Poor Fit:</strong> Deep cleaning service for a house that hasnt been cleaned in a while or for clients who live outside of your normal travel range</p>



<p>To quickly quote professional cleaning services for houses of all sizes, some house cleaning companies establish prices based on a room rate. This refers to the number of bedrooms and bathrooms that will be cleaned.</p>



<p>Calculate your total house cleaning amount using this room rate formula, which assumes a 1-bedroom, 1-bathroom home. Then, adjust the additional room fee as needed:</p>



<p><strong>Price per room</strong> = 100 + (# of extra bathrooms x $20) + (# of extra bedrooms x $10)</p>



<p>If a home has more bedrooms, it may have larger common areas as well, like the kitchen and living room. Remember that when youre calculating room rates for homes with 4+ bedrooms.</p>


	</div>
</section><!-- ./wp-block-jobber-academy-content -->

	class="
		wp-block-jobber-t3-text-cta
		t3
		
		 t3-margin-top-sm line--narrow-width narrow-width
		cta-size--tiny
		cta-style--default
		
		
	"
	
	data-size="tiny"
>
	<div class="wp-block-jobber-t3-text-cta__wrapper">

				<div class="wp-block-jobber-t3-text-cta__body">
					
										<p>Want an easier way to price jobs? <a href="#calculator">Try our free house cleaning cost calculator</a></p>

									</div>

<section
	class="wp-block-jobber-academy-featured-content t3 line--narrow-width
	t3-margin-top-sm
	
	list-columns--one
	"
	
>
	<div class="wp-block-jobber-academy-featured-content__content">
		

<h2 class="wp-block-heading">Pricing considerations for your house cleaning services</h2>



<p>No matter which strategy you choose to set your prices, there are several data points youll always need. These numbers are cost of labor, cost of materials, overhead and equipment, and profit margin.&nbsp;</p>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li><strong>Labor:</strong> Labor charges refer to your hourly rate and that of your team members. Multiply your set hourly rate by the number of cleaners to get a bare minimum charge for a job.<br></li>



<li><strong>Cost of materials</strong>: In your cleaning business, this total might include cleaning products, tools, special chemicals, protective equipment (gloves and masks), or uniforms.</li>
</ul>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li><strong>Overhead</strong>: Overhead includes some operational expenses like taxes, gas for traveling to and from locations, <a href="https://www.getjobber.com/academy/cleaning/cleaning-business-insurance/">cleaning insurance</a>, and <a href="https://www.getjobber.com/academy/cleaning/cleaning-ads-ideas-and-examples/">cleaning business advertising</a>. These expenses arent necessarily attributed to specific jobs and clients, but they ensure that you can maintain your business.<br></li>



<li><strong>Profit margin</strong>: Profit margin is a percentage that you hope to make or take home after other expenses are accounted for. Profit also ensures that you and your team members get paid based on a healthy cost of living.</li>
</ul>



<p>Some elements, like the cost of materials, can change frequently. For instance, buying cleaning supplies in bulk or at wholesale helps reduce supply costs.&nbsp;</p>



<p>Kimberly Towers, owner of <a href="https://www.theredrosemn.com/">The Red Rose</a>, considers the following when pricing her services:</p>



<p><em>The rationale we have behind our pricing and services is what we pay our people to do the job, the cost of the products, equipment, and then the cost of things like our scheduling systems, or uniforms, or things that we have in place on the job that makes The Red Rose what they are.</em></p>



<p>At other times, you might want to increase certain elements. This could be true if you want to <a href="https://www.getjobber.com/academy/cleaning/how-to-sell-house-cleaning-services/">expand your marketing</a> (increase your overhead) or ramp up profit (increase your margin) based on the broader market.</p>



<p><strong>READ MORE:</strong> <a href="https://www.getjobber.com/academy/cleaning/is-a-cleaning-business-profitable/">Is a cleaning business profitable?</a></p>


	</div>
</section><!-- ./wp-block-jobber-academy-featured-content -->


<section
	class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content t3 line--narrow-width
		  t3-margin-top-sm
		  
		  list-columns--one
		  "
	
>
	<div class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content__content">
		

<h2 class="wp-block-heading">Make a cleaning service price sheet for customers</h2>



<p>As you talk to potential customers, youll often need a fast way to share your prices and services with them. Thats where a cleaning services pricing sheet comes in.</p>



<p>On a price sheet, you can highlight the cost of all your services, from small projects to full deep cleans. Not only does this help you maintain consistency, but it also helps your customers visualize their budget. When youre <a href="https://www.getjobber.com/free-tools/proposal-template/cleaning/">proposing a new cleaning job</a>, simply glance at your price sheet or have your future customers do the same.</p>



<p>Heres one example of a residential cleaning price sheet based on projected home size:</p>



<figure class="wp-block-table"><table class="has-fixed-layout"><thead><tr><th class="has-text-align-center" data-align="center"><strong>Type of residence</strong></th><th class="has-text-align-center" data-align="center"><strong>Estimated cleaning cost</strong></th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td class="has-text-align-center" data-align="center">Studio  1BD/BA apartment</td><td class="has-text-align-center" data-align="center">$75-150</td></tr><tr><td class="has-text-align-center" data-align="center">Single family  2BD/2BA home</td><td class="has-text-align-center" data-align="center">$150-200</td></tr><tr><td class="has-text-align-center" data-align="center">Single family  3BD/3BA home</td><td class="has-text-align-center" data-align="center">$200-300</td></tr><tr><td class="has-text-align-center" data-align="center">Single family  3,500+ sq. feet</td><td class="has-text-align-center" data-align="center">Custom quote upon request</td></tr></tbody></table></figure>



<p><em><strong>Pro Tip</strong>:</em> Pricing estimates are even easier to manage when you use <a href="https://www.getjobber.com/industries/cleaning-business-software/">cleaning business software</a>. Keep a digital record of estimated costs, including set fees and optional add-ons, and let your clients easily agree to the work.</p>


	</div>
</section><!-- ./wp-block-jobber-academy-content -->


<section
	class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content t3 line--narrow-width
		  t3-margin-top-sm
		  
		  list-columns--one
		  u-anchor-offset"
	id="factors"
>
	<div class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content__content">
		

<h2 class="wp-block-heading">Factors that affect cleaning service pricing</h2>



<p>As a business owner, remember to keep an open mind about your prices, services, and even your customer base. Flexibility will allow you to adapt, even when trends, overhead expenses, and other factors are beyond your control.<br><br>These are some of the most common factors that could influence how much to charge for home cleaning services:</p>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li><strong>Home sizes</strong>: The larger the home, the more you can expect to charge. You can determine home size based on square footage or the number of rooms. When planning your business, its wise to have a mix of home and project sizes to diversify.<br></li>



<li><strong>Home condition</strong>: When a home is in poor shape, it will need more elbow grease to meet top cleaning standards. Regardless of condition, always invoice for your time and effort. Additionally, you might charge more for homes with pets since pet hair or damage can require extra cleaning time.<br></li>



<li><strong>Home location:</strong> If you have to travel a long distance, charge more to cover time and gas for vehicles. You can also schedule clients in the same area on the same day or use <a href="https://www.getjobber.com/academy/what-is-route-optimization/">route optimization</a> to cut down on commutes.<br></li>



<li><strong>Local demand:</strong> Check your <a href="https://getjobber.com/academy/service-area/">service area</a>s going rate for residential cleaning to ensure you arent over- or undercharging. Even when theres high competition, you can stand out by offering in-demand services that other providers dont perform.<br></li>



<li><strong>Ideal clients</strong>: Make sure your rate is affordable for your ideal client while promoting the quality of the work you do. While you shouldnt stereotype your clients, you should become familiar with their budget and how much theyre willing to pay for good value.<br></li>



<li><strong>Cleaning frequency</strong>: The more time and effort required for a cleaning jobfor example, a deep clean versus regular weekly cleaningthe more you should charge. You might not have recurring work from one move-out cleaning job.<br></li>



<li><strong>Experience level: </strong>A more experienced cleaner can charge a premium based on their training, skills, and experience. If youre less experienced or working to build a reputation, wait to charge a higher rate. With client testimonials and more jobs under your belt, youll soon be able to responsibly increase prices.</li>
</ul>


	</div>
</section><!-- ./wp-block-jobber-academy-content -->


<section
	class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content t3 line--narrow-width

	id="when-to-adjust"
>
	<div class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content__content">
		

<h3 class="wp-block-heading">When to adjust your cleaning prices</h3>



<p>Hourly and one-time service rates may change over time. When it comes to your business, making new price adjustments often depends on your specific services and business goals.</p>



<p>Here are a few scenarios in which its acceptable or smart to reframe your pricing structure:</p>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li>A requested cleaning job is outside of your normal scope of work (i.e., a client has a mold or mildew problem that you normally dont handle)</li>



<li>A cleaning project requires more work than your initial terms of service stated</li>



<li>The home or job site is outside of your local region, requiring more travel and gas</li>



<li>Youre testing a marketing strategy by offering a group rate to a particular neighborhood or group of homes</li>



<li>You want to offer discounts or special rates to repeat clients or referrals</li>



<li>Youve had to drastically change your workforce (making several new hires or having multiple team members leave at one time)</li>
</ul>


	</div>
</section><!-- ./wp-block-jobber-academy-content -->

<section
	class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content t3 line--narrow-width
		  t3-margin-top-sm
		  
		  list-columns--one
		  "
	
>
	<div class="wp-block-jobber-academy-content__content">
		

<p>Introducing price changes can be tricky, but most customers expect small changes over time.&nbsp;</p>



<p><strong>LEARN MORE</strong>: <a href="https://www.getjobber.com/academy/price-increase-letter-sample/">How to write a price increase letter for customers (with free template)</a></p>



<p><em><strong>Pro Tip</strong>: </em>If you want to establish a predictable <a href="https://www.getjobber.com/academy/cleaning/how-to-get-cleaning-contracts/">cleaning contract</a>, perform an initial cleaning before signing. This step lets you know how much work to expect each time and ensures that youre not locked in at a lower rate or longer cleaning time than you planned for.</p>



<p>By now, youve learned that there are a range of pricing methods you can use to establish house cleaning prices. Specialty services, transparent pricing sheets, and flexibility can help you adapt and excel.</p>



<p>As you grow, remember to revisit your pricing strategy to make sure its in alignment with your costs, availability, and profit goals. By being proactive, youll attract more cleaning clients and set yourself up for long-term success.</p>


	</div>
</section><!-- ./wp-block-jobber-academy-content -->
